            Taking on a Billionaire Landlord in the Twin Cities
           </a>
           <span class="paywall-key">
           </span>

           <div class="home-title-large">
            <a href="https://www.yesmagazine.org/health-happiness/2020/06/02/coronavirus-mental-health-data">
             The Mental Toll On Us All
            </a>
            <span class="paywall-key">
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="home-excerpt-large">
            As the coronavirus upends lives, another public health crisis arises. New research shows eight times more people are under serious mental distress now.
           </div>
           <div class="home-author-small">
            <span>
             <a href="https://www.yesmagazine.org/authors/jeane-marie-twenge/">
              Jean M. Twenge
             </a>

           <div class="home-title-large">
            <a href="https://www.yesmagazine.org/economy/2020/04/30/coronavirus-aftermath">
             90% Don’t Want to Return to the Way We Were
            </a>
            <span class="paywall-key">
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="home-excerpt-large">
            What should happen in the aftermath of the coronavirus?
           </div>

           <div class="home-title-large">
            <a href="https://www.yesmagazine.org/health-happiness/2020/03/16/coronavirus-south-korea">
             South Korea Reverses Coronavirus Rates
            </a>
            <span class="paywall-key">
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="home-excerpt-large">
            How did they do it? With extensive countermeasures such as free and quick testing, South Korea has slowed the spread of the virus and on March 14 reported more recoveries than new infections.
           </div>
           <div class="home-author-small">
            <span>
             <a href="https://www.yesmagazine.org/authors/tracy-matsue-loeffelholz/">

                // if cookie is set, hide email signup cta on load
                if (cta_cookie) {
                  $('.newsletter-signup-dnd').addClass('hidden');
                }

                // when email signup cta is submitted check to see if it's successful and set cookie if so
                $cta_wrapper = $('.newsletter-signup-dnd');
                $('.newsletter-signup-dnd form, .pum-content form').on('submit', function(){
                  // wait 6 seconds to ensure XHR request completes before checking for success class
                  setTimeout(function(){
                  if ( $(document).find('.newsletter-signup-dnd .wpcf7-mail-sent-ok, .pum-content .wpcf7-mail-sent-ok').length ) {
                    docCookies.setItem(CTA_COOKIE_NAME, 'viewed', 'Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT', '/');
                    $cta_wrapper.addClass('hidden');
                    $('.pum-active, #pum-' + pop_id).addClass('hidden');
                  }
                }, 6000);

              });

                $('.email-updates-footer-wrapper button:not(.red)').click(function (){
                   $('.email-updates-footer-wrapper').toggleClass('active')                   
                });     
                //$('.email-updates-footer-wrapper').addClass('active');
                
                //Close on scroll on non-touch devices only
                if ($('html').hasClass('no-touch')) {
                    var el = $(window);
                        lastY = el.scrollTop();    
                        el.on('scroll', function() {
                        var currY = el.scrollTop();
                            //y = (currY > lastY) ? 'down' : ((currY === lastY) ? 'none' : 'up');
                            if (currY > lastY) {
                                //if($('.email-updates-footer-wrapper').hasClass('active')) {
                                    $('.email-updates-footer-wrapper').removeClass('active');
                                //}
                            }
                        lastY = currY;
                    });
                }
            });
  </script>

if(typeof mutation.addedNodes[i].getElementsByClassName!=='function'){continue}
images=mutation.addedNodes[i].getElementsByTagName('img');is_image=mutation.addedNodes[i].tagName=="IMG";iframes=mutation.addedNodes[i].getElementsByTagName('iframe');is_iframe=mutation.addedNodes[i].tagName=="IFRAME";rocket_lazy=mutation.addedNodes[i].getElementsByClassName('rocket-lazyload');image_count+=images.length;iframe_count+=iframes.length;rocketlazy_count+=rocket_lazy.length;if(is_image){image_count+=1}
if(is_iframe){iframe_count+=1}}});if(image_count>0||iframe_count>0||rocketlazy_count>0){lazyLoadInstance.update()}});var b=document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];var config={childList:!0,subtree:!0};observer.observe(b,config)}},!1)
  </script>

  <script>
   function lazyLoadThumb(e){var t='<img src="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/ID/hqdefault.jpg" alt="" width="480" height="360">',a='<div class="play"></div>';return t.replace("ID",e)+a}function lazyLoadYoutubeIframe(){var e=document.createElement("iframe"),t="ID?autoplay=1";t+=0===this.dataset.query.length?'':'&'+this.dataset.query;e.setAttribute("src",t.replace("ID",this.dataset.src)),e.setAttribute("frameborder","0"),e.setAttribute("allowfullscreen","1"),e.setAttribute("allow", "accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture"),this.parentNode.replaceChild(e,this)}document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){var e,t,a=document.getElementsByClassName("rll-youtube-player");for(t=0;t<a.length;t++)e=document.createElement("div"),e.setAttribute("data-id",a[t].dataset.id),e.setAttribute("data-query", a[t].dataset.query),e.setAttribute("data-src", a[t].dataset.src),e.innerHTML=lazyLoadThumb(a[t].dataset.id),e.onclick=lazyLoadYoutubeIframe,a[t].appendChild(e)});

  <script>
   $(window).on('load', function() {
        $('#mobile-header .menu-toggle').on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var aria = $('#menu-top-menu-main-1').attr('aria-hidden');

            if (aria == 'false') {
                $('.navigation-search').addClass('search_box');
            } else {
                $('.navigation-search').removeClass('search_box');
            }
        });
    });
